NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

has converted to Hinduism with the name of
S. SAKTHIVEL MURUGAN on 25th March 2012.
RS. MARIA DARCES.

#578 Anna Nagar, Vennaimalaipatty, Kadhaparai(Po), Karur-639 006.
We hereby declare that Mr. K.N. Sivakumar son of T.R. Nallasamy, No.24, Bharathi Nagar, Vaiyapuri Nagar (PO),
Karur-639 002, is relieved from Q PVC BAGS with effect from 01-05-2012 as per Partnership Dissolution Deed.
The New Partnership Deed has been enclosed here with and Mr. N. Balasubramani, son of T. Nagarajan,
No. 30/1, Anna Colony Main Road, Kongu Nagar, Vengamadu, Karur-6 and Mrs. B. Shanthi, wife of N. Balasubramani,
No. 30/1, Anna Colony Main Road, Kongu Nagar, Vengamadu, Karur-6 are continuing as Partners and running this firm in the
same permises and in the same name.
The relieving partner Mr.K.N. Sivakumar son of T.R. Nallasamy does not have any legal rights and
responsibilities in the companys Assets and Liabilities.

Karur,
7th March 2013.
